at verdun , in 1916 , over a 300day period , 700 , 000 people were killed , so about 2 , 000 a day .	在verdun , 1916年 , 一個300天以來 , 70萬人死亡 , 所以每天大約2000人死亡 。
if you roll it forward 20thcentury security into the second world war , you see the battle of stalingrad , 300 days , 2 million people killed .	如果你前進到20世紀 , 安全進入第二次世界大戰 , 你會看到斯大林格勒保衛戰 , 300天內有200萬人被殺 。
we go into the cold war , and we continue to try and build walls .	我們進入冷戰 , 繼續建造圍牆 。
we go from the trench warfare of the first world war to the maginot line of the second world war , and then we go into the cold war , the iron curtain , the berlin wall .	我們從一戰的壕溝 , 到二戰的馬其頓防線 , 然後進入冷戰 , 鐵幕 , 柏林牆 。
my thesis for us today is , instead of building walls to create security , we need to build bridges .	我今天的主題是 , 與其建造牆壁來創造安全 , 我們需要建造橋樑 。
this is a famous bridge in europe .	這是歐洲一座有名的橋
it's the bridge over the drina river , the subject of a novel by ivo andrić , and it talks about how , in that very troubled part of europe and the balkans , over time there's been enormous building of walls .	它就在drina河上 , 是作家ivoandrich的小說的主題 , 這部小說講述了如何在歐洲和巴爾幹地區最動盪的部分 , 經過一段時間 , 已經被大量的牆築起 。
more recently , in the last decade , we begin to see these communities start , hesitatingly , to come together .	近期 , 在過去十年 , 我們開始看到這些社區開始 , 盡管有些猶豫不決地團結在一起 。
i would argue , again , opensource security is about connecting the international , the interagency , the privatepublic , and lashing it together with strategic communication , largely in social networks .	我想再次重申 , 開放式安全是關于國際的 , 國際的 , 跨部門的 , 私人的和公共的 , 並且通過戰略性交流 , 在社交網上聯系在一起 。
so let me talk a little bit about why we need to do that , because our global commons is under attack in a variety of ways , and none of the sources of threat to the global commons will be solved by building walls .	讓我來談談為什麼我們需要那樣做 , 因為我們的公有物受到攻擊 , 被各種方式侵襲 , 且沒有任何威脅能被通過築牆來解決 。
now , i'm a sailor , obviously .	現在 , 顯然我是個水手 ,
this is a ship , a liner , clipping through the indian ocean .	這是一艘船 , 一條線從印度洋上滑過 ,
what's wrong with this picture ?	這張照片有什麼問題 ?
it's got concertina wire along the sides of it .	在這個船上有蛇網環繞 。
that's to prevent pirates from attacking it .	就是為了防止海盜攻擊
piracy is a very active threat today around the world . this is in the indian ocean .	海盜是現今全世界都非常活躍的威脅 。 這是在印度洋 。
piracy is also very active in the strait of malacca .	海盜也在馬斯加的海峽很活躍
it's active in the gulf of guinea .	在幾內亞灣是活躍的
we see it in the caribbean .	我們在加勒比海看到的
it's a $10billionayear discontinuity in the global transport system .	在全球交通運輸系統中 , 價值一百億年的不連續性
last year , at this time , there were 20 vessels , 500 mariners held hostage .	去年 , 此時有20艘船 , 500名船員被綁架爲人質 。
this is an attack on the global commons .	這是對全球公有物的攻擊 。
we need to think about how to address it .	我們需要考慮如何處理它 。
let's shift to a different kind of sea , the cyber sea .	咱們轉到另一種海洋 , 網絡海洋 。
here are photographs of two young men .	這是兩位年輕男子的照片 。
at the moment , they're incarcerated .	此刻 , 他們被監禁著 。
they conducted a credit card fraud that netted them over 10 billion dollars .	他們做了一個信用卡詐騙案 , 淨金超過100億美元 。
this is part of cybercrime which is a $2trillionayear discontinuity in the global economy .	這是全球經濟2兆美元損失的網絡犯罪的一部分 。
two trillion a year .	兩萬億一年 。
that's just under the gdp of great britain .	這僅僅是在英國的國內生產總值之下 。
so this cyber sea , which we know endlessly is the fundamental piece of radical openness , is very much under threat as well .	所以網絡大海 , 我們深知是網絡開放最基本的因素 , 也正在受到威脅 。
another thing i worry about in the global commons is the threat posed by trafficking , by the movement of narcotics , opium , here coming out of afghanistan through europe over to the united states .	另一件我擔心的事 , 是人口販賣所帶來的威脅 , 也就是麻醉劑 , 鴉片等毒品移動 , 從阿富汗穿越歐洲 , 到美國 。
we worry about cocaine coming from the andean ridge north .	我們擔心從andeanridge北部運過來的可卡因 。
we worry about the movement of illegal weapons and trafficking . above all , perhaps , we worry about human trafficking , and the awful cost of it .	我們擔心非法武器的運輸 。 最重要的是 , 我們擔心人力的運輸 , 以及它的糟糕代價 。
trafficking moves largely at sea but in other parts of the global commons .	大體上 , 人口販賣的移動主要是在海上 , 但在全球公有物的其他地方 。
this is a photograph , and i wish i could tell you that this is a very hightech piece of us navy gear that we're using to stop the trafficking .	這是一張照片 , 我真希望我能告訴你這是一個非常高科技的美國海軍武器用來阻止販賣人口 。
the bad news is , this is a semisubmersible run by drug cartels .	壞消息是 , 這是一個販毒組織的半潛水的設備 。
it was built in the jungles of south america .	建造於南美的叢林中 ,
we caught it with that lowtech raft — — and it was carrying six tons of cocaine .	我們用那個低科技的架構逮捕了它 , 它正裝載著六噸的可卡因 。
crew of four . sophisticated communications sweep .	四個船員 , 精良的通信內容掃蕩
this kind of trafficking , in narcotics , in humans , in weapons , god forbid , in weapons of mass destruction , is part of the threat to the global commons .	這種販賣行為 , 包括毒品、人、武器 , 禁止大規模殺傷性武器的上帝 , 是全球公有物的威脅的一部分 。
and let's pull it together in afghanistan today .	讓我們現在一起在阿富汗 。
this is a field of poppies in afghanistan .	這是阿富汗的一個花盆田
eighty to 90 percent of the world's poppy , opium and heroin , comes out of afghanistan .	全世界80%到90%的小馬 , 鴉片和海洛因來自阿富汗 。
we also see there , of course , terrorism .	我們當然也看到了恐怖主義
this is where al qaeda is staged from .	這就是基地組織建立的地方 。
we also see a very strong insurgency embedded there .	我們也看到一個強烈的叛亂就嵌在了那裡 。
so this terrorism concern is also part of the global commons , and what we must address .	所以恐怖主義的擔憂也是全球公有物的一部分 , 我們必須解決的是什麼 。
so here we are , 21st century .	所以 , 在21世紀 ,
we know our 20thcentury tools are not going to work .	我們知道我們20世紀的工具是行不通的
what should we do ?	我們該怎麼做 ?
i would argue that we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我認為我們不能僅僅依靠槍支 , 來提供安全 。
we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我們不能僅僅依靠槍支 , 來提供安全 。
we will need the application of military force .	我們需要軍事力量的應用 。
when we do it , we must do it well , and competently .	當我們這樣做的時候 , 我們必須做得很好 , 而且要能幹 。
but my thesis is , opensource security is about international , interagency , privatepublic connection pulled together by this idea of strategic communication on the internet .	但我的論點是 , 開放式安全是關于國際的 , 跨部門的 , 私人和公共的聯繫 , 通過互聯網上的戰略溝通的想法聯繫在一起 。
let me give you a couple of examples of how this works in a positive way .	讓我給你幾個例子 , 看看它是如何以正面的方式運作的 。
this is afghanistan . these are afghan soldiers .	這是阿富汗 , 這些是阿富汗士兵 。
they are all holding books .	他們都拿著書 。
you should say , " that's odd . i thought i read that this demographic , young men and women in their 20s and 30s , is largely illiterate in afghanistan . "	你應該說 , " 這真是奇怪 。 我想我曾讀到過這個在20 , 30多歲的年輕人 , 主要是不識字的阿富汗 。 "
you would be correct .	你是對的 。
eightyfive percent cannot read when they enter the security forces of afghanistan .	當他們進入安全部隊的時候 , 85%是無法閱讀的 。
why ? because the taliban withheld education during the period of time in which these men and women would have learned to read .	為什麼 ? 因為塔利班在這些男人女人要學會閱讀的時期 , 能夠接受教育 。
so the question is , so , why are they all standing there holding books ?	所以問題是 , 為什麼他們都站在那裏 ? 拿著書站在那裏 ?
the answer is , we are teaching them to read in literacy courses by nato in partnership with private sector entities , in partnership with development agencies .	答案是 , 我們在教導他們閱讀 , 通過北約組織的課程 , 通過和私營機構合作 , 與發展機構合作 。
we've taught well over 200 , 000 afghan security forces to read and write at a basic level .	我們已經教了超過二十萬的阿富汗安全部隊士兵用基本的角度去讀和寫 。
when you can read and write in afghanistan , you will typically put a pen in your pocket .	當你能在阿富汗讀寫 , 你通常會在你的口袋裏放一支筆 。
at the ceremonies , when these young men and women graduate , they take that pen with great pride , and put it in their pocket .	在頒獎典禮上 , 當這些年輕男女畢業時 , 他們很驕傲的拿出筆 , 放在他們的口袋裡 。
this is bringing together international — there are 50 nations involved in this mission — interagency — these development agencies — and privatepublic , to take on this kind of security .	這也使得國際化進步有50個國家跨部門、私人和公共機構聯合起來共同承擔這類安全
now , we are also teaching them combat skills , of course , but i would argue , opensource security means connecting in ways that create longer lasting security effect .	當然 , 我們也教他們戰鬥技能 , 但我想說 , 開放式安全意味著爲創造更持久的安全而聯繫在一起 。
this is a us navy warship .	這是美國海軍戰艦 。
it's called the comfort .	叫做comfort號 。
there's a sister ship called the mercy .	有一艘姐妹船 , 叫做mercy號 。
they are hospital ships .	他們是一艘醫院船 。
this one , the comfort , operates throughout the caribbean and the coast of south america conducting patient treatments .	這一個 , 舒適度 , 在整個加勒比海和南美海岸營運 , 進行病人的治療 。
on a typical cruise , they'll do 400 , 000 patient treatments .	通常 , 他們會進行40萬個治療 ,
it is crewed not strictly by military but by a combination of humanitarian organizations: operation hope , project smile .	船員不是嚴格地從軍 , 而是人道組織組成的 。 人道主義組織:希望、計劃微笑 。
other organizations send volunteers .	其他組織送來志願者 。
interagency physicians come out .	跨年齡的醫師出來 ,
they're all part of this .	他們都是這方面的一部分 。
to give you one example of the impact this can have , this little boy , eight years old , walked with his mother two days to come to the eye clinic put on by the comfort .	舉個例子來說明這會帶來什麼衝擊 , 這個小男孩 , 八歲 , 和他的母親走了兩天 , 去看安慰號上的眼科診所 。
when he was fitted , over his extremely myopic eyes , he suddenly looked up and said , " mama , veo el mundo . "	當他被安裝在極度神秘的眼睛上 , 他突然抬頭 , 說: 「 媽媽 , veoelmundo 。 」
" mom , i see the world . "	" 媽媽 , 我看到世界了 。 "
multiply this by 400 , 000 patient treatments , this privatepublic collaboration with security forces , and you begin to see the power of creating security in a very different way .	把這個乘以40萬個病患治療的數量 , 這個私人和公共的合作關係 , 同時加上安全力量 , 你就會開始看到以截然不同的方式創造安全 。
here you see baseball players .	這裡你可以看到棒球選手
can you pick out the two us army soldiers in this photograph ?	你能在照片中挑出兩名美國軍人嗎 ?
they are the two young men on either side of these young boys . this is part of a series of baseball clinics , where we have explored collaboration between major league baseball , the department of state , who sets up the diplomatic piece of this , military baseball players , who are real soldiers with real skills but participate in this mission , and they put on clinics throughout latin america and the caribbean , in honduras , in nicaragua , in all of the central american and caribbean nations where baseball is so popular , and it creates security .	他們是這兩個年輕男孩的兩邊的年輕人 。 這是棒球診所的一部分 , 在這裏我們探索了棒球聯盟 , 國務院成立了這個組織 , 軍事棒球選手 , 他們是真正的軍人 , 但他們參與了這個任務 , 他們開到了拉丁美洲和加勒比 , 開到了洪都拉斯 , 開到了洪都拉瓜 , 開到了所有中美洲和加勒比 , 開到了所有中美洲和加勒比的棒球聯盟 , 他們創造了安全局 。
it shows role models to young men and women about fitness and about life that i would argue help create security for us .	它顯示出年輕人對健身和生活的榜樣 , 而我認為它能為我們創造安全 。
another aspect of this partnership is in disaster relief .	這夥伴的另一面是在災難救援中
this is a us air force helicopter participating after the tsunami in 2004 which killed 250 , 000 people .	這是美國空軍的直升機 , 它參加了2004年海嘯殺死250 , 000人的活動 。
in each of these major disasters — the tsunami in 2004 , 250 , 000 dead , the kashmiri earthquake in pakistan , 2005 , 85 , 000 dead , the haitian earthquake , about 300 , 000 dead , more recently the awful earthquaketsunami combination which struck japan and its nuclear industry — in all of these instances , we see partnerships between international actors , interagency , privatepublic working with security forces to respond to this kind of natural disaster .	在所有的大災難中2004年海嘯 , 250000死 , 2005年巴基斯坦地震 , 85000死 , 海地地震 , 300000死 , 還有最近的對于日本核子產業的地震海嘯雙重打擊在所有這些例子中 , 我們看到了國際間 , 跨部門 , 跨部門 , 公私結合的合作 , 和公私結合這種自然災害 。
so these are examples of this idea of opensource security .	這些都是開放式安全理念的例子
we tie it together , increasingly , by doing things like this .	我們將它綁在一起 , 漸漸地 , 藉由像這樣的事情做 。
now , you're looking at this thinking , " ah , admiral , these must be sea lanes of communication , or these might be fiber optic cables . "	現在 , 你看到這個 , 應該在想 , 「 啊 , 司法 , 這些一定是通信電纜 , 或者是光纖電纜 。 」
no . this is a graphic of the world according to twitter .	不 , 這是一個twitter公司發的世界地圖
purple are tweets . green are geolocation .	紫色是推特 。 綠色是地理位置 。
white is the synthesis .	白色是綜合 。
it's a perfect evocation of that great population survey , the six largest nations in the world in descending order: china , india , facebook , the united states , twitter and indonesia .	一個完美的革命就是人口量調查顯示世界上六大國依次是下級數的中國 , 印度 , 臉書 , 美國 , twitter和印尼 。
why do we want to get in these nets ?	為什麼我們要用這些蚊帳
why do we want to be involved ?	我們為什麼想要參與 ?
we talked earlier about the arab spring , and the power of all this .	我們之前討論過阿拉伯之春及這一切的力量
i'll give you another example , and it's how you move this message .	我再舉一個例子 , 就是你如何移動這個訊息 。
i gave a talk like this in london a while back about this point . i said , as i say to all of you , i'm on facebook . friend me .	我在倫敦發表一個像這個的演講 。 我對你們說 , 我在facebook上 , 加我好友吧 。
got a little laugh from the audience .	觀眾笑了起來 。
there was an article which was run by ap , on the wire .	曾經有一篇文章由ap負責主導 , 在鋼索上
got picked up in two places in the world: finland and indonesia .	世界上有兩個地方 , 芬蘭和印尼 ,
the headline was: nato admiral needs friends .	標題是:北約司令需要朋友 。
and the story was a catalyst , and the next morning i had hundreds of facebook friend requests from indonesians and finns , mostly saying , " admiral , we heard you need a friend , and oh , by the way , what is nato ? "	而這個故事是一個催化劑 , 隔天早上我就有了數百個facebook好友的請求 , 來自印尼和芬蘭 , 大多數都會說: " 司令 , 我們聽說你需要朋友 , 哦 , 還有 , nato是什麽 ? "
yeah , we laugh , but this is how we move the message , and moving that message is how we connect international , interagency , privatepublic , and these social nets to help create security .	是啊 , 我們笑了 , 但這就是我們如何移動訊息 , 移動那訊息 , 就是我們如何連結國際 , 跨部門 , 私人和公共和私人和這些社會網 , 以協助創造安全 。
now , let me hit a somber note .	現在 , 讓我點擊一個嚴肅的消息 。
this is a photograph of a brave british soldier .	這張照片是一位勇敢的英國士兵 。
he's in the scots guards .	他在蘇格蘭衛隊
he's standing the watch in helmand , in southern afghanistan .	他站在赫爾曼的手錶 , 在阿富汗南部 。
i put him here to remind us , i would not want anyone to leave the room thinking that we do not need capable , competent militaries who can create real military effect .	我把他放到這裡來提醒我們 , 我不想讓任何人離開這間屋子 , 只想著我們不需要能力 , 能力強的軍隊就可以創造真正的軍事效應 。
that is the core of who we are and what we do , and we do it to protect freedom , freedom of speech , all the things we treasure in our societies .	這是我們作為和作為的核心 , 我們為了保護自由 , 言論自由 , 所有我們在社會裡珍視的事物 。
but , you know , life is not an onandoff switch .	但 , 你知道 , 人生並不是開機的開關 。
you don't have to have a military that is either in hard combat or is in the barracks .	你不需要有一支不是在戰鬥中 , 就是在營房裡 。
i would argue life is a rheostat .	我會說 , 人生就像個變電器 。
you have to dial it in , and as i think about how we create security in this 21st century , there will be times when we will apply hard power in true war and crisis , but there will be many instances , as we've talked about today , where our militaries can be part of creating 21stcentury security , international , interagency , privatepublic , connected with competent communication .	你得要把事情做進去 , 且 , 就像我在思考的21世紀 , 我們要如何創造安全 , 在真正的戰爭和危機中 , 會有好幾次 , 但會有許多案例 , 如我們今天所談到的 , 我們的軍隊可以成為21世紀安全的一部分 , 國際 , 跨部門 , 公私結合的一部分 , 連結上了有能力的溝通 。
i would close by saying that we heard earlier today about wikipedia . i use wikipedia all the time to look up facts , and as all of you appreciate , wikipedia is not created by 12 brilliant people locked in a room writing articles .	我最後要說的是 , 今天早些時候 , 我們都聽過維基百科 。 我經常用維基百科查一些事實 , 就像在座各位所體會到的 , 維基百科並不是由12個聰明的人把自己關在房間裡寫文章所創造的 。
wikipedia , every day , is tens of thousands of people inputting information , and every day millions of people withdrawing that information .	維基百科 , 每天都有成千上萬的人在輸入資訊 , 每天有數百萬人在提取那些資訊 。
it's a perfect image for the fundamental point that no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	這是個完美的圖像 , 對於我們之中沒有一個人能像大家一起思考那樣聰明 。
no one person , no one alliance , no one nation , no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	沒有一個人 , 沒有一個聯盟 , 沒有一個國家 , 任何人都沒有像我們一起思考一樣聰明 。
the vision statement of wikipedia is very simple: a world in which every human being can freely share in the sum of all knowledge .	維基的觀點非常簡單每個人類都能自由共享所有知識
my thesis for you is that by combining international , interagency , privatepublic , strategic communication , together , in this 21st century , we can create the sum of all security .	我給你們的論點是 , 藉由結合國際 , 多部門 , 公私力量 , 戰略性的溝通 , 在21世紀 , 我們就能創造出所有安全的總和 。
thank you very much . thank you . thank you .	非常感謝 。 謝謝 。 謝謝 。
